       function validatePassword(pw) {
          // return /^(?=3D.*[A-Za-z])(?=3D.*\d)[A-Za-z\d]{5,}$/.test(pw);
          // return /^(?=3D.*[0-9])(?=3D.*[!@#$%^&*])[a-zA-Z0-9!@#$%^&*]{6,=
16}$/.test(pw);
         var checkSpecial =3D /[*@!#%&()^~{}]+/.test(pw),
        checkUpper =3D /[A-Z]+/.test(pw),
        checkLower =3D /[a-z]+/.test(pw),
        r =3D false;

        if (checkUpper && checkLower && checkSpecial) {
            r =3D true;
        }

        return r;


       }
